&lt;p&gt;Rate limit is one request per second.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-103-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.3 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated &lt;strong&gt;RequestMandateNotification&lt;/strong&gt; schema to include new &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; codes &lt;strong&gt;MAMC, MAMD&lt;/strong&gt; &amp;amp; &lt;strong&gt;MAMX&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated &lt;strong&gt;RequestMandateNotification&lt;/strong&gt; schema to include the amend mandate bilateral request, refer to &lt;strong&gt;details&lt;/strong&gt; object. Applies when &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; code = &lt;strong&gt;MAMC, MAMD&lt;/strong&gt; &amp;amp; &lt;strong&gt;MAMX&lt;/strong&gt;  &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated &lt;strong&gt;MandateNotification&lt;/strong&gt; schema to include the reason why a bilateral request was declined by the Payer, refer to &lt;strong&gt;resolution_event&lt;/strong&gt; object. Applies when &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; code = &lt;strong&gt;MAMD &amp;amp; MCRD&lt;/strong&gt;  &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated &lt;strong&gt;RequestQueryNotification&lt;/strong&gt; to support migrated DDRs&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-102-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.2 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated descriptions from &amp;quot;Payee&amp;quot; to &amp;quot;Biller&amp;quot;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h4 id=&quot;release-101-changes&quot;&gt;Release 1.0.1 changes:&lt;/h4&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;List of mandate attributes amended by Payer can be included in &lt;strong&gt;RequestMandateNotification&lt;/strong&gt; schema, refer to &lt;strong&gt;details&lt;/strong&gt; object.  Applies when &lt;strong&gt;trigger = MAMN&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY bzkQTM"><p>Fileactive Self-Service Testing API. </p>
<p>Rate limit is one request per second.</p>
<h4 id="release-103-changes">Release 1.0.3 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated <strong>RequestMandateNotification</strong> schema to include new <strong>trigger</strong> codes <strong>MAMC, MAMD</strong> &amp; <strong>MAMX</strong></li>
<li>Updated <strong>RequestMandateNotification</strong> schema to include the amend mandate bilateral request, refer to <strong>details</strong> object. Applies when <strong>trigger</strong> code = <strong>MAMC, MAMD</strong> &amp; <strong>MAMX</strong>  </li>
<li>Updated <strong>MandateNotification</strong> schema to include the reason why a bilateral request was declined by the Payer, refer to <strong>resolution_event</strong> object. Applies when <strong>trigger</strong> code = <strong>MAMD &amp; MCRD</strong>  </li>
<li>Updated <strong>RequestQueryNotification</strong> to support migrated DDRs</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-102-changes">Release 1.0.2 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Updated descriptions from &quot;Payee&quot; to &quot;Biller&quot;.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="release-101-changes">Release 1.0.1 changes:</h4>
<ul>
<li>List of mandate attributes amended by Payer can be included in <strong>RequestMandateNotification</strong> schema, refer to <strong>details</strong> object.  Applies when <strong>trigger = MAMN</strong>.</li>
</ul>

&lt;table&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Code&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Name&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Description&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;CMPL&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Completed&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;This status represents the following situations:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;A bilateral action that has been confirmed.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;A unilateral action has been performed.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;A port that has been finalised.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;DECL&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Declined&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Action has been declined.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;TIMO&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;TimedOut&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Action was created bilaterally and has now timed out.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Enumeration of the states that a mandate action can have.</p>
<table><tr><th>Code</th><th>Name</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td>CMPL</td><td>Completed</td><td><p>This status represents the following situations:</p><ul><li>A bilateral action that has been confirmed.</li><li>A unilateral action has been performed.</li><li>A port that has been finalised.</li></ul></td></tr><tr><td>DECL</td><td>Declined</td><td>Action has been declined.</td></tr><tr><td>TIMO</td><td>TimedOut</td><td>Action was created bilaterally and has now timed out.</td></tr></table></div></div></div></td></tr><tr class=""><td kind="field" title="resolution_event" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy sc-jiaSqj cqoAxn hfWKVF gIkRoy"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><button aria-label="expand resolution_event"><span class="property-name">resolution_event</span><svg class="sc-eTNRI jIsRbK" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">object</span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-jgraLO itHPsH iUxudT"> (<!-- -->MandateActionResolutionEvent1<!-- -->) </span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Specification of the resolution event for a mandate action.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Specification of the resolution event for a mandate action.</p>
</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="last "><td kind="field" title="details" class="sc-hABBmJ sc-fHejqy sc-jiaSqj cqoAxn hfWKVF gIkRoy"><span class="sc-ifyrAs hIHfpT"></span><button aria-label="expand details"><span class="property-name">details</span><svg class="sc-eTNRI jIsRbK" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 24 24" x="0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" y="0" aria-hidden="true"><polygon points="17.3 8.3 12 13.6 6.7 8.3 5.3 9.7 12 16.4 18.7 9.7 "></polygon></svg></button></td><td class="sc-blmEgr berbbf"><div><div><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-kZOsHZ itHPsH iSyacY"></span><span class="sc-gUjWJS sc-iLXxbI itHPsH gfdSsP">MandateAmendmentRequest (object) or MandateAmendmentRequestBilat (object) or MandateStatusChangeDetails (object)</span></div> <div><div html="&lt;p&gt;Details of an action performed on a mandate: &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Unilateral Amendment initiated by Payer &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Bilateral Amendment initiated by Biller &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Status Change initiated by Payer&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property descriptions&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;amendment&lt;/strong&gt; - Mandate amendment details provided in the request, &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; = &amp;#39;MAMN&amp;#39;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;bilateral_amendment&lt;/strong&gt; - Mandate amendment details provided in the request, &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; =&amp;#39;MAMC&amp;#39;, &amp;#39;MAMD&amp;#39; &amp;amp; &amp;#39;MAMX&amp;#39;. &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;status_change&lt;/strong&gt; - Mandate status change details provided in the request, &lt;strong&gt;trigger&lt;/strong&gt; =&amp;#39;MSCH&amp;#39;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
" class="sc-iKOmoZ sc-cCzLxZ WVNwY hrWnEm"><p>Details of an action performed on a mandate: </p>
<ul>
<li>Unilateral Amendment initiated by Payer </li>
<li>Bilateral Amendment initiated by Biller </li>
<li>Status Change initiated by Payer</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Property descriptions</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>amendment</strong> - Mandate amendment details provided in the request, <strong>trigger</strong> = &#39;MAMN&#39;.</li>
<li><strong>bilateral_amendment</strong> - Mandate amendment details provided in the request, <strong>trigger</strong> =&#39;MAMC&#39;, &#39;MAMD&#39; &amp; &#39;MAMX&#39;. </li>
<li><strong>status_change</strong> - Mandate status change details provided in the request, <strong>trigger</strong> =&#39;MSCH&#39;.</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="sc-jTQCzO sc-gLLuof imiXRU jGdkPR"><div class="sc-jPQKUW cycbrK"><div class="sc-hVcFVo jeLSWq"><div class="sc-cSxRuM fOJBdW"><div
